‚úÖ SETUP COMPLETE!

The RAG pipeline is ready to use!

Try these commands:

  # Query with retrieval only
  docker compose run --rm rag-pipeline query "How do I use StandardScaler?"

  # Query with answer generation (LLM)
  docker compose run --rm rag-pipeline query "How do I use StandardScaler?" --generate

  # More examples
  docker compose run --rm rag-pipeline query "What is PCA?" --generate
  docker compose run --rm rag-pipeline query "How to handle missing values?" --generate

To stop services:
  docker compose down

To clean everything:
  docker compose down -v
  ./scripts/clean.sh
